This is to inform every student that I.S.T.E of Sardar Beant Singh State University, Gurdaspur is going to conduct *Scien-O-Darshan*  event in TEQFEST-2K22

⚙️⚙️⚙️⚙️⚙️⚙️⚙️⚙️⚙️⚙️⚙️
*RULES*
👉🏻The exhibit/project may include
o	working model to explain a concept, principle or a process.
👉🏻	an indigenous design of a machine/device.
👉🏻an innovative/inexpensive design or technique.
👉🏻	application of basic principles of Science/Technology.
👉🏻Scheme/design of a device or machine to reduce production cost.
o	Investigation based study.
👉🏻There should be a team of 2 students and no teams are allowed more than 2 members.
